Would you like to read a detailed review of Canva? As it's one of the tools I love using. I am also writing my first ebook using canva and publish it soon on my site you can download it is free.&nbsp; Let's start the review.</span></p><p><span style=\"font-family: Frank Ruhl Libre;\">Canva has a web version and also a mobile app</span></p><h3 style=\"text-align: left;\"><span style=\"font-family: Frank Ruhl Libre;\">What is Canva?</span></h3><p><span style=\"font-family: Frank Ruhl Libre;\">Canva is a free graphic design web application that allows you to create invitations, business cards, flyers, lesson plans, banners, and more using professionally designed templates. You can upload your own photos from your computer or from Google Drive, and add them to Canva's templates using a simple drag-and-drop interface. It's like having a basic version of Photoshop that doesn't require Graphic designing knowledge to use. It’s best for nongraphic designers.</span></p><h3 style=\"text-align: left;\"><span style=\"font-family: Frank Ruhl Libre;\">Who is Canva best suited for?</span></h3><p><span style=\"font-family: Frank Ruhl Libre;\">Canva is a great tool for small business owners, online entrepreneurs, and marketers who don’t have the time and want to edit quickly.</span></p><p><span style=\"font-family: Frank Ruhl Libre;\">To create sophisticated graphics, a tool such as Photoshop can is ideal. To use it, you’ll need to learn its hundreds of features, get familiar with the software, and it’s best to have a good background in design, too.</span></p><p><span style=\"font-family: Frank Ruhl Libre;\">Also running the latest version of Photoshop you need a high-end computer.</span></p><p><span style=\"font-family: Frank Ruhl Libre;\">So here&nbsp; Canva takes place, with Canva you can do all that with drag-and-drop feature. It’s also easier to use and free. Also an even-more-affordable paid version is available for $12.95 per month.</span></p><h3 style=\"text-align: left;\"><span style=\"font-family: Frank Ruhl Libre;\">Free vs Pro vs Enterprise Pricing plan</span></h3><p><span style=\"font-family: Frank Ruhl Libre;\">The product is available in three plans: Free, Pro ($12.99/month per user or&nbsp; $119.99/year for up to 5 people), and Enterprise ($30 per user per month, minimum 25 people).</span></p><h3 style=\"text-align: left;\"><span style=\"font-family: Frank Ruhl Libre;\">Free plan Features</span></h3><p></p><ul style=\"text-align: storage</span></li></ul><p></p><h3 style=\"text-align: left;\"><span style=\"font-family: Frank Ruhl Libre;\">Pro Plan Features&nbsp;</span></h3><p></p><ul style=\"text-align: left;\"><li><span designs infinitely with Magic Resize</span></li><li><span style=\"font-family: Frank Ruhl Libre;\">Save designs as templates for your team to use</span></li><li><span style=\"font-family: Frank Ruhl plus:</span></li><li><span style=\"font-family: Frank Ruhl Libre;\">Establish your brand's visual identity with logos, colors and fonts across multiple Brand Kits</span></li><li><span style=\"font-family: Frank Ruhl Libre;\">Control your team's access to apps, graphics, logos, colors and fonts with brand controls</span></li><li><span style=\"font-family: Frank Ruhl Libre;\">Built-in workflows to get approval on your designs</span></li><li><span style=\"font-family: Frank Ruhl Libre;\">Set which elements your team can edit and stay on brand with template locking</span></li><li><span style=\"font-family: Frank Ruhl Libre;\">Unlimited Storage</span></li><li><span style=\"font-family: Frank Ruhl Libre;\">Log in with single-sign on (SSO) and have access to 24/7 Enterprise-level support.</span></li></ul><p></p><h3 style=\"text-align: left;\"><span style=\"font-family: Frank Ruhl Libre;\">How to Use Canva?</span></h3><p><span style=\"font-family: Frank Ruhl Libre;\">To get started on Canva, you will need to create an account by providing your email address, Google, Facebook or Apple credentials. You will then choose your account type between student, teacher, small business, large company, non-profit, or personal. Based on your choice of account type, templates will be recommended to you.</span></p><p><span style=\"font-family: Frank Ruhl Libre;\">You can sign up for a free trial of Canva Pro, or you can start with the free version to get a sense of whether it’s the right graphic design tool for your needs.</span></p><h3 style=\"text-align: left;\"><span style=\"font-family: Frank Ruhl Libre;\">Designing with Canva</span></h3><div><div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\"><a href=\"https://blogger.googleusercontent.com/img/a/AVvXsEgM7YZbpEWXuX7McOKgqVQgrWlabYMSo3a4U9zch0MoomYWl4xBhgZrVjiZKA9hMBEkEL-5IkdFFkw7rotiewBPKDjunpoe6eBXwmG_rk7Ntkw0l4h-bdBMY5LJtS_QFWWkauczX7J4wI5aMMPmHD3nKre-xTEzdLvVVgx5IC5lEAbNpIgSB6kEMRO-iw=s1280\" style=\"margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;\"><img alt=\"canva\" border=\"0\" data-original-height=\"870\" data-original-width=\"1280\" height=\"436\" src=\"https://blogger.googleusercontent.com/img/a/AVvXsEgM7YZbpEWXuX7McOKgqVQgrWlabYMSo3a4U9zch0MoomYWl4xBhgZrVjiZKA9hMBEkEL-5IkdFFkw7rotiewBPKDjunpoe6eBXwmG_rk7Ntkw0l4h-bdBMY5LJtS_QFWWkauczX7J4wI5aMMPmHD3nKre-xTEzdLvVVgx5IC5lEAbNpIgSB6kEMRO-iw=w640-h436\" title=\"canva\" width=\"640\" /></a></div><br /><span style=\"font-family: Frank Ruhl Libre;\"><br /></span></div><p><span style=\"font-family: Frank Ruhl Libre;\">When you sign up for an account, Canva will suggest different post types to choose from. Based on the type of account you set up&nbsp; you'll be able to see templates categorized by the following categories: social media posts, documents, presentations, marketing, events, ads, launch your business, build your online brand, etc.</span></p><p><span style=\"font-family: Frank Ruhl Libre;\">&nbsp;Start by choosing a template for your post or searching for something more specific. Search by social network name to see a list of post types on each network.</span></p><h3 style=\"text-align: left;\"><span style=\"font-family: Frank Ruhl Libre;\">Templates</span></h3><div><div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\"><a href=\"https://blogger.googleusercontent.com/img/a/AVvXsEimJ6jOhTnmaFvrB_VTjmU4f5D4AqXjy65hqYROJW4_z_-EN0phhYBAoCpgD5iq2ICEF19CE6CS1o41joiTQDR12n-trPkotc4gGOggwyf2qpLR5G8pHkXd6DszzjsvJ_OtRZFE5vAUw81Gvv3kr_gdmA_JhhBjSpMDkj1lBWJb1uJeVbPsqwUKgLgMoQ=s1280\" style=\"margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;\"><img alt=\"canva templates\" border=\"0\" data-original-height=\"882\" data-original-width=\"1280\" height=\"442\" src=\"https://blogger.googleusercontent.com/img/a/AVvXsEimJ6jOhTnmaFvrB_VTjmU4f5D4AqXjy65hqYROJW4_z_-EN0phhYBAoCpgD5iq2ICEF19CE6CS1o41joiTQDR12n-trPkotc4gGOggwyf2qpLR5G8pHkXd6DszzjsvJ_OtRZFE5vAUw81Gvv3kr_gdmA_JhhBjSpMDkj1lBWJb1uJeVbPsqwUKgLgMoQ=w640-h442\" title=\"canva templates\" width=\"640\" /></a></div><br /><span style=\"font-family: Frank Ruhl Libre;\"><br /></span></div><p><span style=\"font-family: Frank Ruhl Libre;\">Next, you can choose a template. Choose from hundreds of templates that are ready to go, with customizable photos, text, and other elements.</span></p><p><span style=\"font-family: Frank Ruhl Libre;\">You can start your design by choosing from a variety of ready-made templates, searching for a template matching your needs, or working with a blank template.</span></p><p><span style=\"font-family: Frank Ruhl Libre;\">&nbsp;Canva has a lot to choose from, so start with a specific search.if you want to create business card just search for it and you will see alot of templates to choose from</span></p><h3 style=\"text-align: left;\"><span style=\"font-family: Frank Ruhl Libre;\">Elements</span></h3><p><span style=\"font-family: Frank Ruhl Libre;\">Inside the Canva designer, the Elements tab gives you access to lines and shapes, graphics, photos, videos, audio, charts, photo frames, and photo grids.The search box on the Elements tab lets you search everything on Canva.</span></p><p></p><div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\"><a href=\"https://blogger.googleusercontent.com/img/a/AVvXsEiMPph53bq8js4qlIL55ERQwzAxyL406RSoDJ10bhJ8iO_mlKHtuaQBKAVr4iLEbJh4xEQW7QOfDXOqV1sbYv3qRdMssBchVFWWFqfANHdeX0461ZaBsX_bsLwrB-ad4OyJFfAu03Jyok1fCMvpR5IiBnFjOxVIYbP9AQe7Zs6NIHKwspoD8hl3unL3Dw=s1280\" style=\"margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;\"><img alt=\"canva elements\" border=\"0\" data-original-height=\"882\" data-original-width=\"1280\" height=\"442\" src=\"https://blogger.googleusercontent.com/img/a/AVvXsEiMPph53bq8js4qlIL55ERQwzAxyL406RSoDJ10bhJ8iO_mlKHtuaQBKAVr4iLEbJh4xEQW7QOfDXOqV1sbYv3qRdMssBchVFWWFqfANHdeX0461ZaBsX_bsLwrB-ad4OyJFfAu03Jyok1fCMvpR5IiBnFjOxVIYbP9AQe7Zs6NIHKwspoD8hl3unL3Dw=w640-h442\" title=\"canva elements\" width=\"640\" /></a></div><span style=\"font-family: Frank Ruhl Libre;\"><br /></span><p></p><p><span style=\"font-family: Frank Ruhl Libre;\">To begin with, Canva has a large library of elements to choose from. To find them, be specific in your search query. You may also want to search in the following tabs to see various elements separately:</span></p><h3 style=\"text-align: left;\"><span style=\"font-family: Frank Ruhl Libre;\">Photos</span></h3><p><span style=\"font-family: Frank Ruhl Libre;\">The Photos tab lets you search for and choose from millions of professional stock photos for your templates.</span></p><p><span style=\"font-family: Frank Ruhl Libre;\">You can replace the photos in our templates to create a new look. This can also make the template more suited to your industry.</span></p><p><span style=\"font-family: Frank Ruhl Libre;\">You can find photos on other stock photography sites like pexel, pixabay and many more or simply upload your own photos.</span></p><p></p><div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\"><a href=\"https://blogger.googleusercontent.com/img/a/AVvXsEhKT6RizHZUEKqQQAV8rZZUDBHG_7b8oD-2jNuEUsf4q2RYa7Nx_QDTVSL7vBWvdi8NWBEyV2sKMtE4MtIFgc5O6ggDlunJMNa8ilfAFIWG3xMWQiqY0BKZFHRxn0151lEbOj-6QykEt28OY8e_0F_WyloPPKbiXLH-h68degeJZzyHZddkSO0Ge-zamA=s1280\" style=\"margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;\"><img alt=\"canva photos\" border=\"0\" data-original-height=\"884\" data-original-width=\"1280\" height=\"442\" src=\"https://blogger.googleusercontent.com/img/a/AVvXsEhKT6RizHZUEKqQQAV8rZZUDBHG_7b8oD-2jNuEUsf4q2RYa7Nx_QDTVSL7vBWvdi8NWBEyV2sKMtE4MtIFgc5O6ggDlunJMNa8ilfAFIWG3xMWQiqY0BKZFHRxn0151lEbOj-6QykEt28OY8e_0F_WyloPPKbiXLH-h68degeJZzyHZddkSO0Ge-zamA=w640-h442\" title=\"canva photos\" width=\"640\" /></a></div><span style=\"font-family: Frank Ruhl Libre;\"><br /></span><p></p><p><span style=\"font-family: Frank Ruhl Libre;\">When you choose an image, Canva’s photo editing features let you adjust the photo’s settings (brightness, contrast, saturation, etc.), crop, or animate it.</span></p><p><span style=\"font-family: Frank Ruhl Libre;\">&nbsp;When you subscribe to Canva Pro, you get access to a number of premium features, including the Background Remover. This feature allows you to remove the background from any stock photo in&nbsp; library or any image you upload.</span></p><h3 style=\"text-align: left;\"><span style=\"font-family: Frank Ruhl Libre;\">Text</span></h3><p><span style=\"font-family: Frank Ruhl Libre;\">The Text tab lets you add headings, normal text, and graphical text to your design.</span></p><p><span style=\"font-family: Frank Ruhl Libre;\">When you click on&nbsp; text, you'll see options to adjust the font, font size, color, format, spacing, and text effects (like shadows).&nbsp;</span></p><p><span style=\"font-family: Frank Ruhl Libre;\">Canva Pro subscribers can choose from a large library of fonts on the Brand Kit or the Styles tab. Enterprise-level controls ensure that visual content remains on-brand, no matter how many people are working on it.</span></p><h3 style=\"text-align: left;\"><span style=\"font-family: Frank Ruhl Libre;\">Audio</span></h3><p><span style=\"font-family: Frank Ruhl Libre;\">Create an animated image or video by adding audio to capture user’s attention in social news feeds.</span></p><p><span style=\"font-family: Frank Ruhl Libre;\">If you want to use audio from another stock site or your own audio tracks, you can upload them in the Uploads tab or from the more option.</span></p><h3 style=\"text-align: left;\"><span style=\"font-family: Frank Ruhl Libre;\">Video</span></h3><p><span style=\"font-family: Frank Ruhl Libre;\">Want to create your own videos? Choose from thousands of stock video clips. You’ll find videos that range upto 2 minutes</span></p><p><span style=\"font-family: Frank Ruhl Libre;\">You can upload your own videos as well as videos from other stock sites in the Uploads tab.&nbsp;</span></p><p><span style=\"font-family: Frank Ruhl Libre;\">Once you have chosen a video, you can use the editing features in Canva to trim the video, flip it, and adjust its transparency.</span></p><h3 style=\"text-align: left;\"><span style=\"font-family: Frank Ruhl Libre;\">Backgrounds</span></h3><p><span style=\"font-family: Frank Ruhl Libre;\">On the Background tab, you’ll find free stock photos to serve as backgrounds on your designs. Change out the background on a template to give it a more personal touch.</span></p><h3 style=\"text-align: left;\"><span style=\"font-family: Frank Ruhl Libre;\">Styles</span></h3><div><div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\"><a href=\"https://blogger.googleusercontent.com/img/a/AVvXsEhBQW4BOkq3UutI4TFJiQlwAkDWDeE_48rdkRxCrVrRMkhw6cDGtZKFruHN-Q54dF9446S6j9Wp-9n914SAde1veZqvCo8ATKX2UuSx-TMYq--zNtB2wkFXdtAOS4q6_1EBVCVz8kfJfo2HT2CA-ModbPaq3a86gMezGir-Vqmvz61ic-tJMfxNmblZMA=s1280\" style=\"margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;\"><img border=\"0\" data-original-height=\"880\" data-original-width=\"1280\" height=\"440\" src=\"https://blogger.googleusercontent.com/img/a/AVvXsEhBQW4BOkq3UutI4TFJiQlwAkDWDeE_48rdkRxCrVrRMkhw6cDGtZKFruHN-Q54dF9446S6j9Wp-9n914SAde1veZqvCo8ATKX2UuSx-TMYq--zNtB2wkFXdtAOS4q6_1EBVCVz8kfJfo2HT2CA-ModbPaq3a86gMezGir-Vqmvz61ic-tJMfxNmblZMA=w640-h440\" width=\"640\" /></a></div><span style=\"font-family: Frank Ruhl Libre;\"><br /></span></div><p><span style=\"font-family: Frank Ruhl Libre;\">The Styles tab lets you quickly change the look and feel of your template with just a click. And if you have a Canva Pro subscription, you can upload your brand’s custom colors and fonts to ensure designs stay on brand.</span></p><h3 style=\"text-align: left;\"><span style=\"font-family: Frank Ruhl Libre;\">Logos</span></h3><p><span style=\"font-family: Frank Ruhl Libre;\">If you have a Canva Pro subscription, you’ll have a Logos tab. Here, you can upload variations of your brand logo to use throughout your designs.</span></p><p><span style=\"font-family: Frank Ruhl Libre;\">With Canva, you can also create your own logos. Note that you cannot trademark a logo with stock content in it.</span></p><h3 style=\"text-align: left;\"><span style=\"font-family: Frank Ruhl Libre;\">Publishing with Canva</span></h3><p><span style=\"font-family: Frank Ruhl Libre;\">With Canva, free users can download and share designs to multiple platforms including Instagram, Facebook, Twitter, LinkedIn, Pinterest, Slack and Tumblr.</span></p><p><span style=\"font-family: Frank Ruhl Libre;\">Canva Pro subscribers can create multiple post formats from one design. For example, you can start by designing an Instagram post, and Canva's Magic Resizer can resize it for other networks, Stories, Reels, and other formats.</span></p><p><span style=\"font-family: Frank Ruhl Libre;\">Canva Pro subscribers can also use Canva’s Content Planner to post content on eight different accounts on Instagram, Facebook, Twitter, LinkedIn, Pinterest, Slack, and Tumblr.</span></p><h3 style=\"text-align: left;\"><span style=\"font-family: Frank Ruhl Libre;\">Canva Team</span></h3><p><span style=\"font-family: Frank Ruhl Libre;\">Canva Pro allows you to work with your team on visual content. Designs can be created inside Canva, and then sent to your team members for approval. Everyone can make comments, edits, revisions, and keep track via the version history.</span></p><h3 style=\"text-align: left;\"><span style=\"font-family: Frank Ruhl Libre;\">Canva Print</span></h3><p><span style=\"font-family: Frank Ruhl Libre;\">When it comes to printing your designs, Canva has you covered. With an extensive selection of printing options, they can turn your designs into anything from banners and wall art to mugs and t-shirts.&nbsp;</span></p><p><span style=\"font-family: Frank Ruhl Libre;\">Canva Print is perfect for any business seeking to make a lasting impression. Create inspiring designs people will want to wear, keep, and share. Hand out custom business cards that leave a lasting impression on customers' minds.</span></p><h3 style=\"text-align: left;\"><span style=\"font-family: Frank Ruhl Libre;\">Canva Apps</span></h3><p><span style=\"font-family: Frank Ruhl Libre;\">The Canva app is available on the Apple App Store and Google Play. The Canva app has earned a 4.9 out of five star rating from over 946.3K Apple users and a 4.5 out of five star rating from over 6,996,708 Google users.</span></p><p><span style=\"font-family: Frank Ruhl Libre;\">In addition to mobile apps, you can use Canva’s integration with other Internet services to add images and text from sources like Google Maps, Emojis, photos from Google Drive and Dropbox, YouTube videos, Flickr photos, Bitmojis, and other popular visual content elements.</span></p><h3 style=\"text-align: left;\"><span style=\"font-family: Frank Ruhl Libre;\">Canva Pros and Cons</span></h3><h3 style=\"text-align: left;\"><span style=\"font-family: Frank Ruhl Libre;\">Pros:</span></h3><p></p><ul style=\"text-align: left;\"><li><span style=\"font-family: Frank Ruhl Libre;\">A user-friendly interface</span></li><li><span style=\"font-family: Frank Ruhl Libre;\">Canva is a great tool for people who want to create professional graphics but don’t have graphic design skills.</span></li><li><span style=\"font-family: Frank Ruhl Libre;\">Hundreds of templates, so you'll never have to start from scratch.</span></li><li><span style=\"font-family: Frank Ruhl Libre;\">Wide variety of templates to fit multiple uses</span></li><li><span style=\"font-family: Frank Ruhl Libre;\">Branding kits to keep your team consistent with the brand colors and fonts</span></li><li><span style=\"font-family: Frank Ruhl Libre;\">Creating visual content on the go</span></li><li><span style=\"font-family: Frank Ruhl Libre;\">You can find royalty free images, audio, and video without having to subscribe to another service.</span></li></ul><p></p><h3 style=\"text-align: left;\"><span style=\"font-family: Frank Ruhl Libre;\">Cons:</span></h3><p></p><ul style=\"text-align: left;\"><li><span style=\"font-family: Frank Ruhl Libre;\">Some professional templates are available for Pro user only</span></li><li><span style=\"font-family: Frank Ruhl Libre;\">Advanced photo editing features like blurring or erasing a specific area are missing.</span></li><li><span style=\"font-family: Frank Ruhl Libre;\">Some elements that fall outside of a design are tricky to retrieve.</span></li><li><span style=\"font-family: Frank Ruhl Libre;\">Features (like Canva presentations) could use some improvement.</span></li><li><span style=\"font-family: Frank Ruhl Libre;\">If you are a regular user of Adobe products, you might find Canva's features limited.</span></li><li><span style=\"font-family: Frank Ruhl Libre;\">Prefers to work with vectors. Especially logos.</span></li><li><span style=\"font-family: Frank Ruhl Libre;\">Expensive enterprise pricing</span></li></ul><p></p><h3 style=\"text-align: left;\"><span style=\"font-family: Frank Ruhl Libre;\">Conclusion</span></h3><p><span style=\"font-family: Frank Ruhl Libre;\">In general, Canva is an excellent tool for those who need simple images for projects. If you are a graphic designer with experience, you will find Canva’s platform lacking in customization and advanced features – particularly vectors. But if you have little design experience, you will find Canva easier to use than advanced graphic design tools like Adobe Photoshop or Illustrator for most projects. If you have any queries let me know in the comments section.</span></p><p><span style=\"font-family: Frank Ruhl Libre;\"><br /></span></p><p><span style=\"font-family: Frank Ruhl Libre;\"><br title=\"Grammarly vs prowritingaid\" width=\"640\" /></a></div></h2><div style=\"text-align: left;\"><span style=\"font-family: Comfortaa;\"><b><span><a name='more'></a></span>ProWritingAid VS Grammarly:<span style=\"color: #3c4043;\"><span style=\"background-color: white; font-size: 14px;\">&nbsp;</span></span></b></span><span style=\"color: #3c4043; font-family: Comfortaa;\"><span style=\"font-size: 14px;\">&nbsp;When it comes to English grammar, there are two Big Players that everyone knows of: the Grammarly and ProWritingAid. but you are wondering which one to choose so here we write a detail article which will help you to choose the best one for you so Let's start</span></span></div><h2 style=\"text-align: left;\"><span style=\"font-family: Comfortaa;\">What is Grammarly?</span></h2><p><span style=\"font-family: Comfortaa;\">Grammarly is a tool that checks for grammatical errors, spelling, and punctuation.it gives you comprehensive feedback on your writing. You can use this tool to proofread and edit articles, blog posts, emails, etc.</span></p><p><span style=\"font-family: Comfortaa;\">Grammarly also detects all types of mistakes, including sentence structure issues and misused words. It also gives you suggestions on style changes, punctuation, spelling, and grammar all are in real-time. The free version covers the basics like identifying grammar and spelling mistakes</span></p><p><span style=\"font-family: Comfortaa;\">whereas the Premium version offers a lot more functionality, it detects plagiarism in your content, suggests word choice, or adds fluency to it.</span></p><p><span style=\"font-family: Comfortaa;\"><br /></span></p><h3 style=\"text-align: left;\"><span style=\"font-family: Comfortaa;\"><b>Features of Grammarly</b></span></h3><p></p><ul style=\"text-align: left;\"><li><span style=\"font-family: Comfortaa;\"><b>Spelling and Word Suggestion:</b> Grammarly detects basic to advance grammatical errors and also help you why this is an error and suggest to you how you can improve it</span></li><li><span style=\"font-family: Comfortaa;\"><b>Create a Personal Dictionary:</b> The Grammarly app allows you to add words to your personal dictionary so that the same mistake isn't highlighted every time you run Grammarly.</span></li><li><span style=\"font-family: Comfortaa;\"><b>Different English Style</b>: Check to spell for American, British, Canadian, and Australian English.</span></li><li><span style=\"font-family: Comfortaa;\"><b>Plagiarism:</b> This feature helps you detect if a text has been plagiarized by comparing it with over eight billion web pages.</span></li><li><span style=\"font-family: Comfortaa;\"><b>Wordiness:</b> This tool will help you check your writing for long and hard-to-read sentences. It also shows you how to shorten sentences so that they are more concise.</span></li><li><span style=\"font-family: Comfortaa;\"><b>Passive Voice:</b> The program also notifies users when passive voice is used too frequently in a document.</span></li><li><span style=\"font-family: Comfortaa;\"><b>Punctuations:</b> This feature flags all incorrect and missing punctuation.</span></li><li><span style=\"font-family: Comfortaa;\"><b>Repetition:</b> The tool provides recommendations for replacing the repeated word.</span></li><li><span style=\"font-family: Comfortaa;\"><b>Proposition:</b> Grammarly identifies misplaced and confused prepositions.</span></li><li><span style=\"font-family: Comfortaa;\"><b>Plugins:</b> It offers Microsoft Word, Microsoft Outlook, and Google Chrome plugins.</span></li></ul><p></p><p><span style=\"font-family: Comfortaa;\"><br /></span></p><h2 style=\"text-align: left;\"><span style=\"font-family: Comfortaa;\">What is ProWritingAid?</span></h2><p><span style=\"font-family: Comfortaa;\">ProWritingAid is a style and grammar checker for content creators and writers. It helps to optimize word choice, punctuation errors, and common grammar mistakes, providing detailed reports to help you improve your writing.&nbsp;</span></p><p><span style=\"font-family: Comfortaa;\">ProWritingAid can be used as an add-on to WordPress, Gmail, and Google Docs. The software also offers helpful articles, videos, quizzes, and explanations to help improve your writing.</span></p><h3 style=\"text-align: left;\"><span style=\"font-family: Comfortaa;\">Features of ProWriting Aid</span></h3><p><span style=\"font-family: Comfortaa;\">Here are some key features of ProWriting Aid:</span></p><p></p><ul style=\"text-align: left;\"><li><span style=\"font-family: Comfortaa;\"><b>Grammar checker and spell checker:</b> This tool helps you to find all grammatical and spelling errors.</span></li><li><span style=\"font-family: Comfortaa;\"><b>Find repeated words:</b>&nbsp; The tool also allows you to search for repeated words and phrases in your content.</span></li><li><span style=\"font-family: Comfortaa;\"><b>Context-sensitive style suggestions:</b>&nbsp; You can find the exact style of writing you intend and suggest if it flows well in your writing.</span></li><li><span style=\"font-family: Comfortaa;\"><b>Check the readability of your content:</b> Pro Writing Aid helps you identify the strengths and weaknesses of your article by pointing out difficult sentences and paragraphs.</span></li><li><span style=\"font-family: Comfortaa;\"><b>Sentence Length: </b>It also indicates the length of your sentences.</span></li><li><span style=\"font-family: Comfortaa;\"><b>Check Grammatical error:</b> It also checks your work for any grammatical errors or typos, as well.</span></li><li><span style=\"font-family: Comfortaa;\"><b>Overused words:</b> As a writer, you might find yourself using the same word repeatedly. ProWritingAid's overused words checker helps you avoid this lazy writing mistake.</span></li><li><span style=\"font-family: Comfortaa;\"><b>Consistency:</b> Check your work for inconsistent usage of open and closed quotation marks.</span></li><li><span style=\"font-family: Comfortaa;\"><b>Echoes:</b> Check your writing for uniformly repetitive words and phrases.</span></li></ul><p></p><h3 style=\"text-align: left;\"><span style=\"font-family: Comfortaa;\">Difference between Grammarly and Pro-Writing Aid</span></h3><p><span style=\"font-family: Comfortaa;\"><b>Grammarly</b> and <b>ProWritingAid</b> are well-known grammar-checking software. However, if you're like most people who can't decide which to use, here are some different points that may be helpful in your decision.</span></p><h3 style=\"text-align: left;\"><span style=\"font-family: Comfortaa;\">Grammarly vs ProWritingAid</span></h3><p></p><ul style=\"text-align: left;\"><li><span style=\"font-family: Comfortaa;\"><b>Grammarly </b>is a writing enhancement tool that offers suggestions for grammar, vocabulary, and syntax whereas <b>ProWritingAid</b> offers world-class grammar and style checking, as well as advanced reports to help you strengthen your writing.</span></li><li><span style=\"font-family: Comfortaa;\"><b>Grammarly</b> provides Android and IOS apps whereas <b>ProWritingAid</b> doesn't have a mobile or IOS app.</span></li><li><span style=\"font-family: Comfortaa;\"><b>Grammarly</b> offers important suggestions about mistakes you've made whereas <b>ProWritingAid</b>&nbsp; shows more suggestions than Grammarly but all recommendations are not accurate</span></li><li><span style=\"font-family: Comfortaa;\"><b>Grammarly</b> has a more friendly UI/UX whereas the ProWritingAid interface is not friendly as Grammarly.</span></li><li><span style=\"font-family: Comfortaa;\"><b>Grammarly</b> is an accurate grammar checker for non-fiction writing whereas <b>ProWritingAid</b> is an accurate grammar checker for fiction writers.</span></li><li><span style=\"font-family: Comfortaa;\"><b>Grammarly</b> finds grammar and punctuation mistakes, whereas <b>ProWritingAid</b> identifies run-on sentences and fragments.</span></li><li><span style=\"font-family: Comfortaa;\"><b>Grammarly</b> provides 24/7 support via submitting a ticket and sending emails. <b>ProWritingAid’s</b> support team is available via email, though the response time is approximately 48 hours.</span></li><li><span style=\"font-family: Comfortaa;\"><b>Grammarly</b> offers many features in its free plan, whereas<b> ProWritingAid</b> offers some basic features in the free plan.</span></li><li><span style=\"font-family: Comfortaa;\"><b>Grammarly </b>does not offer much feedback on big picture writing; <b>ProWritingAid</b> offers complete feedback on big picture writing.</span></li><li><span style=\"font-family: Comfortaa;\"><b>Grammarly</b> is a better option for accuracy, whereas <b>ProWritingAid</b> is better for handling fragmented sentences and dialogue. It can be quite useful for fiction writers.</span></li></ul><p></p><h2 style=\"text-align: left;\"><span style=\"font-family: Comfortaa;\">ProWritingAid VS Grammarly: Pricing Difference</span></h2><p></p><ul style=\"text-align: left;\"><li><span style=\"font-family: Comfortaa;\">ProWritingAid comes with three pricing structures. The full-year cost of ProWritingAid is $79, while its lifetime plans cost $339. You also can opt for a monthly plan of $20.</span></li><li><span style=\"font-family: Comfortaa;\">Grammarly offers a Premium subscription for $30/month for a monthly plan&nbsp; $20/month for quarterly and $12/month for an annual subscription.</span></li><li><span style=\"font-family: Comfortaa;\">The Business plan costs $12.50 per month for each member of your company.</span></li></ul><p></p><h2 style=\"text-align: left;\"><span style=\"font-family: Comfortaa;\">ProWritingAid vs Grammarly – Pros and Cons</span></h2><h3 style=\"text-align: left;\"><span spelling.</span></li><li><span style=\"font-family: Comfortaa;\">Offers most features in the free plan</span></li><li><span style=\"font-family: Comfortaa;\">Allows you to edit a document without punctuation, grammar, and spelling errors.</span></li><li><span style=\"font-family: Comfortaa;\">Allows you to make changes to a document without altering its formatting.</span></li><li><span style=\"font-family: Comfortaa;\">Helps users improve vocabulary</span></li><li><span style=\"font-family: Comfortaa;\">User-friendly interface</span></li><li><span style=\"font-family: Comfortaa;\">Browser extensions and MS word add-ons</span></li><li><span style=\"font-family: Comfortaa;\">Available on all major devices and platforms</span></li><li><span style=\"font-family: tools.</span></li></ul><p></p><h3 style=\"text-align: left;\"><span style=\"font-family: Comfortaa;\">ProWritingAid Cons</span></h3><p></p><ul style=\"text-align: left;\"><li><span offers no mobile app for Android or iOS devices.</span></li><li><span style=\"font-family: Comfortaa;\">Plagiarism checker is only available in premium plans.</span></li><li><span style=\"font-family: Comfortaa;\">All recommendations are not accurate</span></li></ul><p></p><h2 style=\"text-align: left;\"><span style=\"font-family: Comfortaa;\">Summarizing the Ginger VS Grammarly: My Recommendation</span></h2><p><span style=\"font-family: Comfortaa;\">As both writing assistants are great in their own way, you need to choose the one that suits you best.</span></p><p></p><ul style=\"text-align: left;\"><li><span style=\"font-family: Comfortaa;\">For example, go for Grammarly&nbsp; if you are a non-fiction writer</span></li><li><span style=\"font-family: Comfortaa;\">Go for ProWritingAid if you are a fiction writer.</span></li><li><span style=\"font-family: Comfortaa;\">ProWritingAid is better at catching errors found in long-form content. However, Grammarly is more suited to short blog posts and other similar tasks.</span></li><li><span style=\"font-family: Comfortaa;\">ProWritingAid helps you clean up your writing by checking for style, structure, and content while Grammarly focuses on grammar and punctuation.</span></li><li><span style=\"font-family: Comfortaa;\">Grammarly has a more friendly UI/UX whereas; ProWritingAid offers complete feedback on big picture writing.</span></li></ul><p></p><p><span style=\"font-family: Comfortaa;\">Both ProWritingAid and Grammarly are awesome writing tools, without a doubt. but as per my experience, Grammarly is a winner here because Grammarly helps you to review and edit your content. Grammarly highlights all the mistakes in your writing within seconds of copying and pasting the content into Grammarly’s editor or using the software’s native feature in other text editors.</span></p><p><span style=\"font-family: Comfortaa;\">Not only does it identify tiny grammatical and spelling errors, it tells you when you overlook punctuations where they are needed. And, beyond its plagiarism-checking capabilities, Grammarly helps you proofread your content. Why is email marketing important?</span></h3><div><span style=\"font-family: Frank Ruhl Libre;\">Email is the marketing tool that helps you&nbsp; create a seamless, connected, frictionless buyer journey. More importantly, email marketing allows you to build relationships with prospects, customers, and past customers. It's your chance to speak&nbsp; to them right in their inbox, at a time that suits them. Along with the right message, email can become one of your most powerful marketing channels.</span></div><h3 style=\"text-align: left;\"><span style=\"font-family: &quot;Frank Ruhl Libre&quot;;\">2. What is benefits of email marketing?</span></h3><div><span style=\"font-family: Frank Ruhl Libre;\">Email marketing is best way for creating long term relationship with your clients, and increasing sales in our company.</span></div><div><span style=\"font-family: Frank Ruhl Libre;\"><br /></span></div><div><span style=\"font-family: Frank Ruhl Libre;\">Benefits of email marketing for bussiness:</span></div><div><ul style=\"text-align: left;\"><li><span style=\"font-family: Frank Ruhl Libre;\">Better brand recognition</span></li><li><span style=\"font-family: Frank Ruhl Libre;\">Statistics of what works best</span></li><li><span style=\"font-family: Frank Ruhl Libre;\">More sales</span></li><li><span style=\"font-family: Frank Ruhl Libre;\">Targeted audience</span></li><li><span style=\"font-family: Frank Ruhl Libre;\">More traffic to your products/services/newsletter</span></li><li><span style=\"font-family: Frank Ruhl Libre;\">Build credibility</span></li></ul></div><div><span style=\"font-family: Frank Ruhl Libre;\">Most&nbsp; bussinesses are using email marketing and making tons of money with email marketing.</span></div><div><span style=\"font-family: Frank Ruhl Libre;\"><br /></span></div><h3 style=\"text-align: left;\"><span style=\"font-family: Frank Ruhl Libre;\">3. What is the simplest day and time to send my marketing emails?</span></h3><div><span style=\"font-family: Frank Ruhl Libre;\"><br /></span></div><div><span style=\"font-family: Frank Ruhl Libre;\">Again, the answer to this question varies from company to company. And again, testing is the way to find out what works best. Typically, weekends and mornings seem to be&nbsp; times when multiple emails are opened, but since your audience may have different habits, it's best to experiment and then use your&nbsp; data to decide.</span></div><div><span style=\"font-family: Frank Ruhl Libre;\"><br /></span></div><h3 style=\"text-align: left;\"><span style=\"font-family: Frank Ruhl Libre;\">&nbsp;4. Which metrics should I be looking at?</span></h3><div><span style=\"font-family: Frank Ruhl Libre;\"><br /></span></div><div><span style=\"font-family: Frank Ruhl Libre;\">The two most important metrics for email marketing are&nbsp; open rate and click-through rate. If your emails aren't opened, subscribers will never see your full marketing message, and if they open them but don't click through to your site, your emails won't convert.</span></div><div><span style=\"font-family: Frank Ruhl Libre;\"><br /></span></div><h3 style=\"text-align: left;\"><span style=\"font-family: Frank Ruhl Libre;\">5. How do I write a decent subject line?</span></h3><div><span style=\"font-family: Frank Ruhl Libre;\"><br /></span></div><div><span style=\"font-family: Frank Ruhl Libre;\">The best subject lines are short and to the point, accurately describing&nbsp; the content of the email, but also catchy and intriguing, so the reader wants to know more. Once Again, this is the perfect place for&nbsp; A/B testing, to see what types of subject lines work best with your audience. Your call to action should be clear and&nbsp; simple. It should be somewhere at the top of your email for those who haven't finished reading the entire email,&nbsp; then repeated&nbsp; at the end for those reading all the way through. It should state exactly what you want subscribers to do, for example \"Click here to download the premium theme for free.</span></div><h3 style=\"text-align: left;\"><span style=\"font-family: Frank Ruhl Libre;\"><br />6. Is email marketing still effective?</span></h3><div><span style=\"font-family: Frank Ruhl Libre;\">Email marketing is one of the most effective ways for a business to reach its customers directly. Think about it. You don't post something on your site&nbsp; hoping people will visit it. You don't even post something on a social media page and hope fans&nbsp; see it. You're sending something straight to each person's inbox, where they'll definitely&nbsp; see it! Even if they don't open it, they'll still see your subject line and business name every time you send an email, so you're still communicating directly with your audience.</span></div><div><span style=\"font-family: Frank Ruhl Libre;\"><br /></span></div><h3 style=\"text-align: left;\"><span style=\"font-family: Frank Ruhl Libre;\">7. However do I grow my email subscribers list? Should i buy an email list or build it myself?</span></h3><div><span style=\"font-family: Frank Ruhl Libre;\">Buying an email list is&nbsp; waste of time &amp; money. These email accounts are unverified and not interested in your brand. The mailing list is useless if your subscribers do not open your emails. There are different ways to grow your mailing list.&nbsp;</span></div><div><span style=\"font-family: Frank Ruhl Libre;\"><br /></span></div><div><span style=\"font-family: Frank Ruhl Libre;\">Give them a free ebook and host it on a landing page where they have to enter the email to download the file and also create a forum page on your website, asks your visitors what questions they might have about your business, and collects email addresses to follow up with them.</span></div><div><span style=\"font-family: Frank Ruhl Libre;\"><br /></span></div><h3 style=\"text-align: left;\"><span style=\"font-family: Frank Ruhl Libre;\">8. How do I prevent audience from unsubscribing?</span></h3><div><span style=\"font-family: Frank Ruhl Libre;\"><br /></span></div><div><span style=\"font-family: Frank Ruhl Libre;\">If the&nbsp; subject line of the email is irrelevant to&nbsp; customers, they will ignore it multiple times. But, if it keeps repeating, they are intercepted and unsubscribed from your emails. So, send relevant emails for the benefit of the customer. Don't send emails that often only focus&nbsp; on sales, offers and discounts.&nbsp;</span></div><div><span style=\"font-family: Frank Ruhl Libre;\">Submit information about your business and offers so you can connect with customers. You can also update them on recent trends in your industry. The basic role of an email is first and foremost to&nbsp; connect with customers, get the most out of this tool.</span></div><div><span style=\"font-family: Frank Ruhl Libre;\"><br /></span></div><h3 style=\"text-align: left;\"><span style=\"font-family: Frank Ruhl Libre;\">9. What is the difference between a cold email and a spam email?</span></h3><div><span style=\"font-family: Frank Ruhl Libre;\"><br /></span></div><div><span style=\"font-family: Frank Ruhl Libre;\">Cold emails are mostly sales emails that are sent with content align to the needs of the recipient. It is usually personalized and includes a business perspective. However, it is still an unsolicited email. And all unsolicited emails are marked as SPAM.&nbsp;</span></div><div><span style=\"font-family: Frank Ruhl Libre;\">Regularly receiving this type of unsolicited email in your users' inboxes, chances are&nbsp; your emails will soon be diverted to&nbsp; spam or junk folders. The most important thing to prevent this from happening is to respect your recipients' choice to opt-out of receiving emails from you. You can add the links to easily unsubscribe. You must be familiar with the CAN-SPAM Act and its regulations.</span></div><div><span style=\"font-family: Frank Ruhl Libre;\"><br /></span></div><h3 style=\"text-align: left;\"><span style=\"font-family: Frank Ruhl Libre;\">10. Where can I find email template?</span></h3><div><span style=\"font-family: Frank Ruhl Libre;\">Almost all email campaign tools provide you with ready-made templates. Whether you use MailChimp or Pardot, you'll get several email templates ready to use.</span></div><div><span style=\"font-family: Frank Ruhl Libre;\">&nbsp;However, if you want to create a template from scratch, you can do so.Most of email campaign tools have option to paste the HTML code of your own design.&nbsp;</span></div><h3 style=\"text-align: left;\"><span style=\"font-family: Frank Ruhl Libre;\"><br />11. What email marketing trend will help marketers succeed in 2022?</span></h3><div><span style=\"font-family: Frank Ruhl Libre;\">Is it a trend to listen to&nbsp; and get to know your customers? I think people realize how bad it feels for a brand or a company to obsess over themselves without knowing their customers personal needs. People who listen empathetically and then provide value based on what they learn will win.</span></div></div><h3 style=\"text-align: left;\"><span style=\"font-family: Frank Ruhl Libre;\"><br /></span><span style=\"font-family: Frank Ruhl Libre;\">Final Saying</span></h3><div><span style=\"font-family: Frank Ruhl Libre;\"><br /></span></div><div><span style=\"font-family: Frank Ruhl Libre;\">&nbsp;You can approach email marketing in different ways. Sellfy provides a customizable storefront where users can display their digital products and embed \"Buy Now\" buttons on their website or blog. Sellfy product pages enable users to showcase their products from different angles with multiple images and previews from Soundcloud, Vimeo, and YouTube. Files of up to 2GB can be uploaded to Sellfy, and the company offers unlimited bandwidth and secure file storage. Users can also embed their entire store or individual project widgets in their site, with the ability to preview how widgets will appear before they are displayed.</span></p><h3 style=\"text-align: left;\"><span style=\"font-family: Comfortaa;\">Features</span></h3><p style=\"text-align: left;\"><span style=\"font-family: Comfortaa; font-weight: normal;\">Sellfy includes:</span></p><h3 style=\"text-align: left;\"><span style=\"font-family: Comfortaa;\">Online Store</span></h3><p><span style=\"font-family: Comfortaa;\"><a href=\"https://get.sellfy.com/crunchhype\" rel=\"nofollow\" target=\"_blank\">Sellfy </a>is a powerful e-commerce platform that helps you personalize your online storefront. You can add your logo, change colors, revise navigation, and edit the layout of your store. Sellfy also allows you to create a full shopping cart so customers can purchase multiple items. And Sellfy gives you the ability to set your language or let customers see a translated version of your store based on their location.</span></p><p><span style=\"font-family: Comfortaa;\"><a href=\"https://get.sellfy.com/crunchhype\" rel=\"nofollow\" target=\"_blank\">Sellfy </a>gives you the option to host your store directly on its platform, add a custom domain to your store, and use it as an embedded storefront on your website. Sellfy also optimizes its store offerings for mobile devices, allowing for a seamless checkout experience.</span></p><h3 style=\"text-align: left;\"><span style=\"font-family: Comfortaa;\">Product hosting</span></h3><p><span style=\"font-family: Comfortaa;\"><a href=\"https://get.sellfy.com/crunchhype\" rel=\"nofollow\" target=\"_blank\">Sellfy </a>allows creators to host all their products and sell all of their digital products on one platform. Sellfy also does not place storage limits on your store but recommends that files be no larger than 5GB. Creators can sell both standard and subscription-based products in any file format that is supported by the online marketplace. Customers can purchase products instantly after making a purchase – there is no waiting period.</span></p><p><span style=\"font-family: Comfortaa;\">You can organize your store by creating your product categories, sorting by any characteristic you choose. Your title, description, and the image will be included on each product page. In this way, customers can immediately evaluate all of your products. You can offer different pricing options for all of your products, including \"pay what you want,\" in which the price is entirely up to the customer. This option allows you to give customers control over the cost of individual items (without a minimum price) or to set pricing minimums—a good option if you're in a competitive market or when you have higher-end products. You can also offer set prices per product as well as free products to help build your store's popularity.</span></p><p><span style=\"font-family: Comfortaa;\">Sellfy is ideal for selling digital content, such as ebooks. But it does not allow you to copyrighted material (that you don't have rights to distribute).</span></p><h3 style=\"text-align: left;\"><span style=\"font-family: Comfortaa;\">Embed options</span></h3><p><span style=\"font-family: Comfortaa;\">Sellfy offers several ways to share your store, enabling you to promote your business on different platforms. Sellfy lets you integrate it with your existing website using \"buy now\" buttons, embed your entire storefront, or embed certain products so you can reach more people. Sellfy also enables you to connect with your Facebook page and YouTube channel, maximizing your visibility.</span></p><h3 style=\"text-align: left;\"><span style=\"font-family: Comfortaa;\">Payments and security</span></h3><p><span style=\"font-family: Comfortaa;\">Sellfy is a simple online platform that allows customers to buy your products directly through your store. Sellfy has two payment processing options: PayPal and Stripe. You will receive instant payments with both of these processors, and your customer data is protected by Sellfy's secure (PCI-compliant) payment security measures. In addition to payment security, Sellfy provides anti-fraud tools to help protect your products including PDF stamping, unique download links, and limited download attempts.</span></p><h3 style=\"text-align: left;\"><span style=\"font-family: Comfortaa;\">Marketing and analytics tools</span></h3><p><span style=\"font-family: Comfortaa;\">The Sellfy platform includes marketing and analytics tools to help you manage your online store. You can send email product updates and collect newsletter subscribers through the platform. With Sellfy, you can also offer discount codes and product upsells, as well as create and track Facebook and Twitter ads for your store. The software's analytics dashboard will help you track your best-performing products, generated revenue, traffic channels, top locations, and overall store performance.</span></p><h3 style=\"text-align: left;\"><span style=\"font-family: Comfortaa;\">Integrations</span></h3><p><span style=\"font-family: Comfortaa;\">To expand functionality and make your e-commerce store run more efficiently, Sellfy offers several integrations. Google Analytics and Webhooks, as well as integrations with Patreon and Facebook Live Chat, are just a few of the options available. Sellfy allows you to connect to Zapier, which gives you access to hundreds of third-party apps, including tools like Mailchimp, Trello, Salesforce, and more.</span></p><h3 style=\"text-align: These include information about your domains, organic keyword analysis, ad keyword, and site traffic.<o:p></o:p></span></p> <p class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin-bottom: 12.0pt; margin-left: 0in; margin-right: 0in; margin-top: 12.0pt; margin: 12pt 0in;\"><span style=\"font-family: Frank Ruhl Libre;\">You'll also find some other options like<o:p></o:p></span></p> <p class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin-bottom: 12.0pt; margin-left: 0in; margin-right: 0in; margin-top: 12.0pt; margin: 12pt 0in;\"></p><ul style=\"text-align: left;\"><li><span style=\"font-family: Frank Ruhl Libre;\">A search bar allows you to enter a domain, keyword, or anything else you wish to explore.</span></li><li><span style=\"font-family: Frank Ruhl Libre;\">A menu on the left side of the page provides quick links to relevant information, including marketing insights, projects, keyword analytics, and more.</span></li><li><span style=\"font-family: Frank Ruhl Libre;\">The customer support resources located directly within the dashboard can be used to communicate with the support team or to learn about other resources such as webinars and blogs.</span></li><li><span style=\"font-family: Frank Ruhl Libre;\">Detailed descriptions of every resource offered. This detail is beneficial for new marketers, who are just starting.</span></li></ul><p></p>       <h4 style=\"break-after: auto; margin-bottom: 15.95pt; margin-left: 0in; margin-right: 0in; margin-top: 15.95pt; margin: 15.95pt 0in; mso-pagination: widow-orphan; page-break-after: auto;\"><span style=\"font-family: Frank Ruhl Libre;\"><span color=\"windowtext\" style=\"mso-bidi-font-style: normal;\">WHO WINS?</span><o:p></o:p></span></h4> <p class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin-bottom: 12.0pt; margin-left: 0in; margin-right: 0in; margin-top: 12.0pt; margin: 12pt 0in;\"><span style=\"font-family: Frank Ruhl Libre;\">Both Ahrefs and SEMrush have user-friendly dashboards, but Ahrefs is less cluttered and easier to navigate. On the other hand, SEMrush offers dozens of extra tools, including access to customer support resources.<o:p></o:p></span></p> <p class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin-bottom: 12.0pt; margin-left: 0in; margin-right: 0in; margin-top: 12.0pt; margin: 12pt 0in;\"><span style=\"font-family: Frank Ruhl Libre;\">When deciding on which dashboard to use, consider what you value in the user interface, and test out both.<o:p></o:p></span></p> <h3 style=\"break-after: auto; margin-bottom: 14.05pt; margin-left: 0in; margin-right: 0in; margin-top: 14.05pt; margin: 14.05pt 0in; mso-pagination: widow-orphan; page-break-after: auto;\"><span style=\"font-family: Frank Ruhl Libre;\"><span color=\"windowtext\">Rank Tracking</span><o:p></o:p></span></h3> <p class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin-bottom: 12.0pt; margin-left: 0in; margin-right: 0in; margin-top: 12.0pt; margin: 12pt 0in;\"><span style=\"font-family: Frank Ruhl Libre;\">If you're looking to track your website's search engine ranking, rank tracking features can help. You can also use them to monitor your competitors.<o:p></o:p></span></p> <p class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin-bottom: 12.0pt; margin-left: 0in; margin-right: 0in; margin-top: 12.0pt; margin: 12pt 0in;\"><span style=\"font-family: Frank Ruhl Libre;\">Let's take a look at Ahrefs vs. SEMrush to see which tool does a better job.<o:p></o:p></span></p> <h2 style=\"margin: 12pt 0in; text-align: left;\"><span style=\"font-family: Frank Ruhl Libre;\">Ahrefs</span></h2><div><div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\"><a href=\"https://blogger.googleusercontent.com/img/a/AVvXsEiwI2EsnhOaR8PPGn03_vC7Rnhyl6hbADM_ilA7IukOAIz0A7SFJDh0Gkj85yqIOJv4gBiiBdfcd_0hy3b7gTYPZhUKQ4eyWLi60IxDA_w-tXRSQ3QkogvhxI1lgvgM59SpOnj8Z6rj9mC_EEBV8k60_c3P4ywhjUD5DKgpM73Vei7qqC7sHIIyVyYXxA=s623\" imageanchor=\"1\" style=\"margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;\"><img alt=\"ahrefs rank tracking\" border=\"0\" data-original-height=\"492\" data-original-width=\"623\" height=\"506\" src=\"https://blogger.googleusercontent.com/img/a/AVvXsEiwI2EsnhOaR8PPGn03_vC7Rnhyl6hbADM_ilA7IukOAIz0A7SFJDh0Gkj85yqIOJv4gBiiBdfcd_0hy3b7gTYPZhUKQ4eyWLi60IxDA_w-tXRSQ3QkogvhxI1lgvgM59SpOnj8Z6rj9mC_EEBV8k60_c3P4ywhjUD5DKgpM73Vei7qqC7sHIIyVyYXxA=w640-h506\" title=\"ahrefs rank tracking\" width=\"640\" /></a></div><br /><span style=\"font-family: Frank Ruhl Libre;\"><br /></span></div><span><!--more--></span> <p class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin-bottom: 12.0pt; margin-left: 0in; margin-right: 0in; margin-top: 12.0pt; margin: 12pt 0in;\"><span style=\"font-family: Frank Ruhl Libre;\">The Ahrefs Rank Tracker is simpler to use. Just type in the domain name and keywords you want to analyze, and it spits out a report showing you the search engine results page (SERP) ranking for each keyword you enter.<o:p></o:p></span></p> <p class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin-bottom: 12.0pt; margin-left: 0in; margin-right: 0in; margin-top: 12.0pt; margin: 12pt 0in;\"><span style=\"font-family: Frank Ruhl Libre;\">Rank Tracker looks at the ranking performance of keywords and compares them with the top rankings for those keywords. Ahrefs also offers:<o:p></o:p></span></p> <p class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin-bottom: 12.0pt; margin-left: 0in; margin-right: 0in; margin-top: 12.0pt; margin: 12pt 0in;\"><span style=\"font-family: Frank Ruhl Libre;\">You'll see metrics that help you understand your visibility, traffic, average position, and keyword difficulty.<o:p></o:p></span></p> <p class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin-bottom: 12.0pt; margin-left: 0in; margin-right: 0in; margin-top: 12.0pt; margin: 12pt 0in;\"><span style=\"font-family: Frank Ruhl Libre;\">It gives you an idea of whether a keyword would be profitable to target or not.<o:p></o:p></span></p> <h4 style=\"break-after: auto; margin-bottom: 15.95pt; margin-left: 0in; margin-right: 0in; margin-top: 15.95pt; margin: 15.95pt 0in; mso-pagination: widow-orphan; page-break-after: auto;\"><span style=\"font-family: Frank Ruhl Libre;\"><span color=\"windowtext\" style=\"mso-bidi-font-style: normal;\">SEMRUSH</span><o:p></o:p></span></h4><div><span style=\"font-family: Frank Ruhl Libre;\"><div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\"><a href=\"https://blogger.googleusercontent.com/img/a/AVvXsEhcPjF5Xp0f_j3LEzL1aOppWxoqdWtxA7kwRMnWHbiSk-_coyrMwWl6kjy3t_sT0TULSm0C6CzC2-xxgTzz_Gp7zDB5uotawo722P-uBuk_Wm1LXyj3W2zKSGIPRazUBmHLGaFWXskZcQGSezKY5yQF07pKF3QYdWIqXyDoNuSvG9Iv8bnR3-fB29VRSA=s352\" imageanchor=\"1\" style=\"margin-left: 1em; margin-left: 0in; margin-right: 0in; margin-top: 12.0pt; margin: 12pt 0in;\"><span style=\"font-family: Frank Ruhl Libre;\">SEMRush offers a tool called Position Tracking. This tool is a project tool—you must set it up as a new project. Below are a few of the most popular features of the SEMrush Position Tracking tool:<o:p></o:p></span></p> <p class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin-bottom: 12.0pt; margin-left: 0in; margin-right: 0in; margin-top: 12.0pt; margin: 12pt 0in;\"><span style=\"font-family: Frank Ruhl Libre;\">All subscribers are given regular data updates and mobile search rankings upon subscribing<o:p></o:p></span></p> <p class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin-bottom: 12.0pt; margin-left: 0in; margin-right: 0in; margin-top: 12.0pt; margin: 12pt 0in;\"><span style=\"font-family: Frank Ruhl Libre;\">The platform provides opportunities to track several SERP features, including Local tracking.<o:p></o:p></span></p> <p class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin-bottom: 12.0pt; margin-left: 0in; margin-right: 0in; margin-top: 12.0pt; margin: 12pt 0in;\"><span style=\"font-family: Frank Ruhl Libre;\">Intuitive reports allow you to track statistics for the pages on your website, as well as the keywords used in those pages.<o:p></o:p></span></p> <p class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin-bottom: 12.0pt; margin-left: 0in; margin-right: 0in; margin-top: 12.0pt; margin: 12pt 0in;\"><span style=\"font-family: Frank Ruhl Libre;\">Identify pages that may be competing with each other using the Cannibalization report.<o:p></o:p></span></p> <h4 style=\"break-after: auto; margin-bottom: 15.95pt; margin-left: 0in; margin-right: 0in; margin-top: 15.95pt; margin: 15.95pt 0in; mso-pagination: widow-orphan; page-break-after: auto;\"><span style=\"font-family: Frank Ruhl Libre;\"><span color=\"windowtext\" style=\"mso-bidi-font-style: normal;\">WHO WINS?</span><o:p></o:p></span></h4> <p class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin-bottom: 12.0pt; margin-left: 0in; margin-right: 0in; margin-top: 12.0pt; margin: 12pt 0in;\"><span style=\"font-family: Frank Ruhl Libre;\">Ahrefs is a more user-friendly option. It takes seconds to enter a domain name and keywords. From there, you can quickly decide whether to proceed with that keyword or figure out how to rank better for other keywords.<o:p></o:p></span></p> <p class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin-bottom: 12.0pt; margin-left: 0in; margin-right: 0in; margin-top: 12.0pt; margin: 12pt 0in;\"><span style=\"font-family: Frank Ruhl Libre;\">SEMrush allows you to check your mobile rankings and ranking updates daily, which is something Ahrefs does not offer. SEMrush also offers social media rankings, a tool you won't find within the Ahrefs platform. Both are good which one do you like let me know in the comment.<o:p></o:p></span></p> <h2 style=\"margin: 12pt 0in; text-align: left;\"><span style=\"font-family: Frank Ruhl Libre;\">Keyword Research</span></h2> <p class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin-bottom: 12.0pt; margin-left: 0in; margin-right: 0in; margin-top: 12.0pt; margin: 12pt 0in;\"><span style=\"font-family: Frank Ruhl Libre;\">Keyword research is closely related to rank tracking, but it's used for deciding which keywords you plan on using for future content rather than those you use now.<o:p></o:p></span></p> <p class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin-bottom: 12.0pt; margin-left: 0in; margin-right: 0in; margin-top: 12.0pt; margin: 12pt 0in;\"><span style=\"font-family: Frank Ruhl Libre;\">When it comes to SEO, keyword research is the most important thing to consider when comparing the two platforms.<o:p></o:p></span></p> <h4 style=\"break-after: auto; margin-bottom: 15.95pt; margin-left: 0in; margin-right: 0in; margin-top: 15.95pt; margin: 15.95pt 0in; mso-pagination: widow-orphan; page-break-after: auto;\"><span style=\"font-family: Frank Ruhl Libre;\"><span color=\"windowtext\" style=\"mso-bidi-font-style: normal;\">AHREFS</span><o:p></o:p></span></h4><div><span style=\"font-family: Frank Ruhl Libre;\"><div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; margin-left: 0in; margin-right: 0in; margin-top: 12.0pt; margin: 12pt 0in;\"><span style=\"font-family: Frank Ruhl Libre;\">The Ahrefs Keyword Explorer provides you with thousands of keyword ideas and filters search results based on the chosen search engine.<o:p></o:p></span></p> <p class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin-bottom: 12.0pt; margin-left: 0in; margin-right: 0in; margin-top: 12.0pt; margin: 12pt 0in;\"><span style=\"font-family: Frank Ruhl Libre;\">Ahrefs supports several features, including:<o:p></o:p></span></p> <p class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin-bottom: 12.0pt; margin-left: 0in; margin-right: 0in; margin-top: 12.0pt; margin: 12pt 0in;\"></p><ul style=\"text-align: left;\"><li><span style=\"font-family: Frank Ruhl Libre;\">It can search multiple keywords in a single search and analyze them together. At SEMrush, you also have this feature in Keyword Overview.</span></li><li><span style=\"font-family: Frank Ruhl Libre;\">Ahrefs has a variety of keywords for different search engines, including Google, YouTube, Amazon, Bing, Yahoo, Yandex, and other search engines.</span></li><li><span style=\"font-family: Frank Ruhl Libre;\">When you click on a keyword, you can see its search volume and keyword difficulty, but also other keywords related to it, which you didn't use.</span></li></ul><p></p>     <h2 style=\"margin: 12pt 0in; text-align: left;\"><span style=\"font-family: Frank Ruhl Libre;\">SEMRUSH</span></h2><div><div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\"><a href=\"https://blogger.googleusercontent.com/img/a/AVvXsEjiBVN83kj79tj3MmwHM5ELWsU9oAx5bZ7Y7znUE1zevmfGZNcshIh-7WzAWu7StXVuAG7wcLTgAzfLSn5wZ-8ur9EQtkjlMb0Tz22Qitnl1iKHq7iSfq3oNr281qY_3jamHUjaSWx2Yl4Q-47dZmgjLyvO9l9LooPjxRLN2eZTZIT0u8awK8ImaZsaoQ=s1672\" imageanchor=\"1\" style=\"margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;\"><img border=\"0\" data-original-height=\"904\" data-original-width=\"1672\" height=\"346\" src=\"https://blogger.googleusercontent.com/img/a/AVvXsEjiBVN83kj79tj3MmwHM5ELWsU9oAx5bZ7Y7znUE1zevmfGZNcshIh-7WzAWu7StXVuAG7wcLTgAzfLSn5wZ-8ur9EQtkjlMb0Tz22Qitnl1iKHq7iSfq3oNr281qY_3jamHUjaSWx2Yl4Q-47dZmgjLyvO9l9LooPjxRLN2eZTZIT0u8awK8ImaZsaoQ=w640-h346\" width=\"640\" /></a></div><br /><span style=\"font-family: Frank Ruhl Libre;\"><br /></span></div><span><!--more--></span> <p class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin-bottom: 12.0pt; margin-left: 0in; margin-right: 0in; margin-top: 12.0pt; margin: 12pt 0in;\"><span style=\"font-family: Frank Ruhl Libre;\">SEMrush's Keyword Magic Tool has over 20 billion keywords for Google. You can type in any keyword you want, and a list of suggested keywords will appear.<o:p></o:p></span></p> <p class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin-bottom: 12.0pt; margin-left: 0in; margin-right: 0in; margin-top: 12.0pt; margin: 12pt 0in;\"><span style=\"font-family: Frank Ruhl Libre;\">The Keyword Magic Tool also lets you to:<o:p></o:p></span></p> <p class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin-bottom: 12.0pt; margin-left: 0in; margin-right: 0in; margin-top: 12.0pt; margin: 12pt 0in;\"></p><ul style=\"text-align: left;\"><li><span style=\"font-family: Frank Ruhl Libre;\">Show performance metrics by keyword</span></li><li><span style=\"font-family: Frank Ruhl Libre;\">Search results are based on both broad and exact keyword matches.</span></li><li><span style=\"font-family: Frank Ruhl Libre;\">Show data like search volume, trends, keyword difficulty, and CPC.</span></li><li><span style=\"font-family: Frank Ruhl Libre;\">Show the first 100 Google search results for any keyword.</span></li><li><span style=\"font-family: Frank Ruhl Libre;\">Identify SERP Features and Questions related to each keyword</span></li><li><span style=\"font-family: Frank Ruhl Libre;\">SEMrush has released a new Keyword Gap Tool that uncovers potentially useful keyword opportunities for you, including both paid and organic keywords.</span></li></ul><p></p>           <h4 style=\"break-after: auto; margin-bottom: 15.95pt; margin-left: 0in; margin-right: 0in; margin-top: 15.95pt; margin: 15.95pt 0in; mso-pagination: widow-orphan; page-break-after: auto;\"><span style=\"font-family: Frank Ruhl Libre;\"><span color=\"windowtext\" style=\"mso-bidi-font-style: normal;\">WHO WINS?</span><o:p></o:p></span></h4> <p class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin-bottom: 12.0pt; margin-left: 0in; margin-right: 0in; margin-top: 12.0pt; margin: 12pt 0in;\"><span style=\"font-family: Frank Ruhl Libre;\">Both of these tools offer keyword research features and allow users to break down complicated tasks into something that can be understood by beginners and advanced users alike.<o:p></o:p></span></p> <p class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin-bottom: 12.0pt; margin-left: 0in; margin-right: 0in; margin-top: 12.0pt; margin: 12pt 0in;\"><span style=\"font-family: Frank Ruhl Libre;\">If you're interested in keyword suggestions, SEMrush appears to have more keyword suggestions than Ahrefs does. It also continues to add new features, like the Keyword Gap tool and SERP Questions recommendations.<o:p></o:p></span></p> <h3 style=\"break-after: auto; margin-bottom: 14.05pt; margin-left: 0in; margin-right: 0in; margin-top: 14.05pt; margin: 14.05pt 0in; mso-pagination: widow-orphan; page-break-after: auto;\"><span style=\"font-family: Frank Ruhl Libre;\"><span color=\"windowtext\">Competitor Analysis</span><o:p></o:p></span></h3> <p class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin-bottom: 12.0pt; margin-left: 0in; margin-right: 0in; margin-top: 12.0pt; margin: 12pt 0in;\"><span style=\"font-family: Frank Ruhl Libre;\">Both platforms offer competitor analysis tools, eliminating the need to come up with keywords off the top of your head. Each tool is useful for finding keywords that will be useful for your competition so you know they will be valuable to you.<o:p></o:p></span></p> <h4 style=\"break-after: auto; margin-bottom: 15.95pt; margin-left: 0in; margin-right: 0in; margin-top: 15.95pt; margin: 15.95pt 0in; mso-pagination: widow-orphan; page-break-after: auto;\"><span style=\"font-family: Frank Ruhl Libre;\"><span color=\"windowtext\" style=\"mso-bidi-font-style: normal;\">AHREFS</span><o:p></o:p></span></h4><div><span style=\"font-family: Frank Ruhl Libre;\"><div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; margin-left: 0in; margin-right: 0in; margin-top: 12.0pt; margin: 12pt 0in;\"><span style=\"font-family: Frank Ruhl Libre;\"><span>Ahrefs' domain comparison tool lets you compare up to five websites (your website and four competitors) side-by-side.it also shows you&nbsp;</span>how your site is ranked against others with metrics such as backlinks, domain ratings, and more.</span></p> <p class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin-bottom: 12.0pt; margin-left: 0in; margin-right: 0in; margin-top: 12.0pt; margin: 12pt 0in;\"><span style=\"font-family: Frank Ruhl Libre;\">Use the Competing Domains section to see a list of your most direct competitors, and explore how many keywords matches your competitors have.<o:p></o:p></span></p> <p class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin-bottom: 12.0pt; There are countless ways to use explosive topics to your advantage as a content creator.&nbsp;</span></div><p><span style=\"font-family: Frank Ruhl Libre;\">Some examples can be:</span></p><p></p><ul style=\"text-align: left;\"><li><span style=\"font-family: Frank Ruhl Libre;\">Use the most popular hashtags and keywords to get inspiration for ideas.</span></li><li><span style=\"font-family: Frank Ruhl Libre;\">&nbsp;Find out what people are talking about in real-time.</span></li><li><span style=\"font-family: Frank Ruhl Libre;\">&nbsp;Find new audiences you may not have known were interested in your topic.</span></li></ul><p></p><p><span style=\"font-family: Frank Ruhl Libre;\">There’s no excuse not to try this website — it’s free and easy to use!</span></p><p><span style=\"font-family: Frank Ruhl Libre;\"><a href=\"https://explodingtopics.com/\" rel=\"nofollow\" target=\"_blank\">Visit Exploding Topics From Here</a></span></p><h3 style=\"text-align: left;\"><span style=\"font-family: Frank Ruhl Libre;\">2. margin-right: auto;\"><span style=\"font-family: Frank Ruhl Libre;\"><img alt=\"Headline Studio\" border=\"0\" data-original-height=\"526\" data-original-width=\"660\" height=\"510\" src=\"https://blogger.googleusercontent.com/img/a/AVvXsEg_BImtXlDG4mY8E1M-s7N9jOu5mCNj4xpeck4f4BjnbBk28ufqx8PrbIGztTVFEjJyPgGYSb1c5Lot3i2FFvoTf9hceIdMZ0q0UlzHwIAgekKDQzenRCFDXjjmCDRGVWcweACwx4TWJNkTkLP3qY4MVhAhzHV_NvX827iVC4Isi_5PY1APma3Q86sKqg=w640-h510\" title=\"Headline Studio\" width=\"640\" /></span></a></td></tr><tr><td class=\"tr-caption\" style=\"text-align: center;\"><span style=\"font-family: Frank Ruhl Libre;\">(Photo Credit:-Headline Studio)</span></td></tr></tbody></table></div><div><span style=\"font-family: Frank Ruhl Libre;\"><br /></span></div><p><span><span style=\"font-family: Frank Ruhl Libre;\"></span></span></p><!--more--><span style=\"font-family: Frank Ruhl Libre;\"><span>Headline Studio allows you to create catchy headlines for your content.&nbsp;</span><span>After writing a title there is data on how often people view articles with similar titles and why they are involved with them.</span></span><p></p><p><span style=\"font-family: Frank Ruhl Libre;\">This is a valuable tool when creating new blog posts because it generates catchy headlines for your blog post to catch a reader’s attention.</span></p><p><a href=\"https://coschedule.com/headline-studio\" rel=\"nofollow\" target=\"_blank\"><span style=\"font-family: Frank Ruhl Libre;\">Visit Headline Studio From Here</span></a></p><h3 style=\"text-align: left;\"><span style=\"font-family: Frank Ruhl Libre;\">3. Answer the public</span></h3><div><table align=\"center\" cellpadding=\"0\" cellspacing=\"0\" class=\"tr-caption-container\" style=\"margin-left: auto; margin-right: auto;\"><tbody><tr><td style=\"text-align: center;\"><a href=\"https://blogger.googleusercontent.com/img/a/AVvXsEhDhwDpmPqs-AfaJNuQH-ZI-fg5MSl8TFMFUQLd0-yFurLMLy_1v49EHto_y9A4sI-vfmW5vmIiGnBC2-LKgXOZDXthDwXBGCrRUkwpEHLI42IjYf7tO35yZH4Ru2EUnAeE_FNLbKeqsUEsFFElGZ1ZfxVH5SyD0VFFstvvN8xUms5oG55piVEgGQ7Zgw=s665\" style=\"margin-left: auto; margin-right: auto;\"><span style=\"font-family: Frank Ruhl Libre;\"><img alt=\"Answer The Public\" border=\"0\" data-original-height=\"657\" data-original-width=\"665\" height=\"632\" src=\"https://blogger.googleusercontent.com/img/a/AVvXsEhDhwDpmPqs-AfaJNuQH-ZI-fg5MSl8TFMFUQLd0-yFurLMLy_1v49EHto_y9A4sI-vfmW5vmIiGnBC2-LKgXOZDXthDwXBGCrRUkwpEHLI42IjYf7tO35yZH4Ru2EUnAeE_FNLbKeqsUEsFFElGZ1ZfxVH5SyD0VFFstvvN8xUms5oG55piVEgGQ7Zgw=w640-h632\" title=\"Answer The Public\" width=\"640\" /></span></a></td></tr><tr><td class=\"tr-caption\" style=\"text-align: center;\"><span style=\"font-family: Frank Ruhl Libre;\">(Photo Credit:- Answer The Public)</span></td></tr></tbody></table><span style=\"font-family: Frank Ruhl Libre;\"><br /></span></div><p><span><span style=\"font-family: Frank Ruhl Libre;\"></span></span></p><!--more--><span style=\"font-family: Frank Ruhl Libre;\">Answer The public is an excellent tool for content creators. It gives you insight into what people are asking on social media sites and communities and lets you guess about topics that matter to your audience. Answer the public allows you to enter a keyword or topic related to your niche and it will show results with popular questions and keywords related to your topic. It's an amazing way to get insights into what people are searching online and allows you to identify topics driven by new blog posts or social media content on platforms like Facebook, Instagram, Youtube, and Twitter as well as the types of questions they ask and&nbsp; also want answers.</span><p></p><p><span style=\"font-family: Frank Ruhl Libre;\"><a href=\"https://answerthepublic.com/\" rel=\"nofollow\" target=\"_blank\">Visit&nbsp;Answer The Public From Here</a></span></p><h3 style=\"text-align: left;\"><span style=\"font-family: Frank Ruhl Libre;\">4. Surfer Seo (SEO Ranking)</span></h3><div><table align=\"center\" cellpadding=\"0\" cellspacing=\"0\" class=\"tr-caption-container\" style=\"margin-left: auto; margin-right: auto;\"><tbody><tr><td style=\"text-align: center;\"><a href=\"https://blogger.googleusercontent.com/img/a/AVvXsEjOUhpQP2O68T9_tM27QAv_umu2RIQxnCSRfjJ9hK0w04j-LEkhxd-7wEhtVKUqTXyCEJZ7agOQFq9A5KBjzwN0g8zyPXwrDMh0RUgUBXjVqKKsSzY_4DleJcS2UA5HeKfev_o7cqESm3Ax0bejSQ48B-889nuJbde7jiVRZ8eTvuf8TrELwgGdjseCZw=s640\" style=\"margin-left: auto; margin-right: auto;\"><span style=\"font-family: Frank Ruhl Libre;\"><img alt=\"Surfer Seo\" border=\"0\" data-original-height=\"400\" data-original-width=\"640\" height=\"400\" src=\"https://blogger.googleusercontent.com/img/a/AVvXsEjOUhpQP2O68T9_tM27QAv_umu2RIQxnCSRfjJ9hK0w04j-LEkhxd-7wEhtVKUqTXyCEJZ7agOQFq9A5KBjzwN0g8zyPXwrDMh0RUgUBXjVqKKsSzY_4DleJcS2UA5HeKfev_o7cqESm3Ax0bejSQ48B-889nuJbde7jiVRZ8eTvuf8TrELwgGdjseCZw=w640-h400\" title=\"Surfer Seo\" width=\"640\" /></span></a></td></tr><tr><td class=\"tr-caption\" style=\"text-align: center;\"><span style=\"font-family: Frank Ruhl Libre;\">(Photo Credit:-Surfer Seo)</span></td></tr></tbody></table><span style=\"font-family: Frank Ruhl Libre;\"><br /><span><br /></span></span></div><p><span><span style=\"font-family: Frank Ruhl Libre;\"></span></span></p><!--more--><span style=\"font-family: Frank Ruhl Libre;\">With this tool, content creators can quickly and easily check the ranking of their websites and those of other competitors. This tool allows you to see how your website compares to others in different categories, including:&nbsp;</span><p></p><p></p><ul style=\"text-align: left;\"><li><span style=\"font-family: Frank Ruhl Libre;\">Rank Potential</span></li><li><span style=\"font-family: Frank Ruhl Libre;\">Organic Search Ranking</span></li></ul><p></p><p><span style=\"font-family: Frank Ruhl Libre;\">Surfer Seo is free and the interface is very friendly. It's a great tool for anyone who wants to do quick competitor research or check their site's rankings at any time.</span></p><p><span style=\"font-family: Frank Ruhl Libre;\"><a href=\"https://surferseo.com/\" rel=\"nofollow\" target=\"_blank\">Visit SurferSeo From Here</a></span></p><h3 style=\"text-align: left;\"><span style=\"font-family: Frank Ruhl Libre;\">5. Canva (Templates/Graphics)</span></h3><div><table align=\"center\" cellpadding=\"0\" cellspacing=\"0\" class=\"tr-caption-container\" style=\"margin-left: auto; margin-right: auto;\"><tbody><tr><td style=\"text-align: center;\"><a href=\"https://blogger.googleusercontent.com/img/a/AVvXsEjHx5hbdU0ZIHY4IGh8jRKSfmbrXldgc6KgR2KC7qI4Hti-fZmxcJqSB4WsQ9xSMc_lAlvczySNLl1aYHA02zu7wzHrAB81ZggyIApoJt3Y3n7-uDMC4-2xmH7X0kzhuMoGwDGhtpAxbuxbB2fWpWrSPsJ1ybyrJaCMbZHADcWkrfGuVuTJkhEzzvx9qQ=s676\" style=\"margin-left: auto; margin-right: auto;\"><span style=\"font-family: Frank Ruhl Libre;\"><img alt=\"Canva\" border=\"0\" data-original-height=\"417\" data-original-width=\"676\" height=\"394\" src=\"https://blogger.googleusercontent.com/img/a/AVvXsEjHx5hbdU0ZIHY4IGh8jRKSfmbrXldgc6KgR2KC7qI4Hti-fZmxcJqSB4WsQ9xSMc_lAlvczySNLl1aYHA02zu7wzHrAB81ZggyIApoJt3Y3n7-uDMC4-2xmH7X0kzhuMoGwDGhtpAxbuxbB2fWpWrSPsJ1ybyrJaCMbZHADcWkrfGuVuTJkhEzzvx9qQ=w640-h394\" title=\"Canva\" width=\"640\" /></span></a></td></tr><tr><td class=\"tr-caption\" style=\"text-align: center;\"><span style=\"font-family: Frank Ruhl Libre;\">(Photo Credit:- Canva)</span></td></tr></tbody></table><span style=\"font-family: Frank Ruhl Libre;\"><br /><br /></span></div><p><span><span style=\"font-family: Frank Ruhl Libre;\"></span></span></p><!--more--><span style=\"font-family: Frank Ruhl Libre;\">Canva is a free graphic design platform that makes it easy to create invitations, business cards, mobile videos, Instagram posts, Instagram stories, flyers, and more with professionally designed templates. You can even upload your photos and drag and drop them into Canva templates. It's like having a basic version of Photoshop. You can also remove background from images with one click.</span><p></p><p><span style=\"font-family: Frank Ruhl Libre;\">Canva offers thousands of free, professionally designed templates that can be customized with just a few clicks. Simply upload your photos to Canva, drag them into the template of your choice, and save the file to your computer.</span></p><p><span style=\"font-family: Frank Ruhl Libre;\">It is free to use for basic use but if you want access to different fonts or more features, then you need to buy a premium plan.</span></p><p><span style=\"font-family: Frank Ruhl Libre;\"><a href=\"https://www.canva.com/\" rel=\"nofollow\" target=\"_blank\">Visit Canva From Here</a></span></p><h3 style=\"text-align: left;\"><span style=\"font-family: Frank Ruhl Libre;\">6. This can help you understand the demographics, interests, and behaviors of your target audience. This information helps determine the direction of your content so that it resonates with them. The most important tools to consider in Facebook Audience Insights are Demographics and Behavior. These two sections provide you with valuable information about your target market, such as their age and from where they belong, how much time they spend on social media per day, what devices they use to access it, etc.</span><p></p><p><span style=\"font-family: Frank Ruhl Libre;\"><br /></span></p><p><span style=\"font-family: Frank Ruhl Libre;\">There is another section of Facebook Audits that is very helpful. This will let you know the interests, hobbies, and activities that people in your target market are most interested in. You can use this information to create content for them about things they will be about as opposed to topics they may not be so keen on.</span></p><p><span style=\"font-family: Frank Ruhl Libre;\"><a href=\"https://www.google.com/search?q=Facebook+Audience+Insights&amp;oq=Facebook+Audience+Insights&amp;aqs=chrome..69i57j69i176j69i58.244j0j4&amp;client=ms-android-transsion-infinix-rev1&amp;sourceid=chrome-mobile&amp;ie=UTF-8\" rel=\"nofollow\" target=\"_blank\"><span>Visit&nbsp;</span>Facebook Audience Insights From Here</a></span></p><h3 style=\"text-align: left;\"><span style=\"font-family: Frank Ruhl Libre;\">7.
